# a
### -a

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-a|*-a]]_.
> ¹ Adjunct
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-a|-a]]_ ("adjective")
### abta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑbtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑbdʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [äbdə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*apta|*apta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ap|*ap]]_ ("lay out, arrange") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Laid out flat; ² Arranged in a particular way
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#abda|abda]]_
### acas
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑtʃɑs]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑdʒʌs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ädʒʌs]

### acok'

### acowmö

> ¹ Six
### acö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑtʃø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑdʒœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ädʒœ]

### -ag

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ag|*-ag]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count smaller land animals that are typically considered edible such as [[K'übi]], flightless birds and big toads
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-on|-on]]_
### agoa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑŋoɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑŋɔʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [äŋɔə]

### bac'ük

### bamay

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#böb|böb]]_
### böta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bøtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bødʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bødə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pütta|*pütta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*püt|*püt]]_ ("paint") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Painted
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#böda|böda]]_
### bötböt
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bøtbøt]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bødbœt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bødbœt]

> ¹ Paint
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#bödböt|bödböt]]_
### bötic
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bøtitʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bødɪtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bødɪtʃ]

### böxök

### byabya

### byako

### cia
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʃiɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʃiʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʃiə]

### cik'em
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʃikʼem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʃikʼɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʃikʼɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cīk'em|*cīk'em]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cīk'|*cīk']]_ ("tip") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Tail; ² Back end
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#jíken|jíken]]_
### cimcim
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʃimtʃim]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʃɪ̃ndʒɪ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʃɪ̃ndʒɪ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cimcim|*cimcim]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ci|*ci]]_ ("red") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ [[Cimcim]], edible red algae cultivated by the Öb
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#jinjin|jinjin]]_, [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#cimcim|cimcim]]_
### cisk'on
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʃiskʼon]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʃiskʼɔ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʃiskʼɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cisk'un|*cisk'un]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ci|*ci]]_ ("red") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sek'u|*sek'u]]_ ("beak") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-en|*-en]]_ ("possessed").
> ¹ [[Cisk'on]], a species of kingfisher with a red beak
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#jískon|jískon]]_
### cita
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʃitɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʃidʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʃidə]

> ¹ To have passed
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#jída|jída]]_
### clogi

### colan
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʃolɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʃolʌ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʃolɔ̃ː]

### c'abet

> ¹ Human singular
### eal

### gilbu
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋilbu]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋiɫbʊ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋewbʊ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gilpū|*gilpū]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gil|*gil]]_ ("moon") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pū|*pū]]_ ("elder sibling").
> ¹ The larger of the two moons of winter
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#göbu|göbu]]_
### gilki
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋilki]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋiɫkɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋewkɪ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gilki|*gilki]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gil|*gil]]_ ("moon") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ki|*ki]]_ ("younger sibling").
> ¹ The smaller of the two moons of winter
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#göki|göki]]_
### gilmö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋilmø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋiɫmœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋewmœ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gilmü|*gilmü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gil|*gil]]_ ("moon") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mü|*mü]]_ ("cycle").
> ¹ A minor month, equal to 10 days
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#gömö|gömö]]_
### gosum
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋosum]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋosʊ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋosʊ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gusūm|*gusūm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sūm|*sūm]]_ ("remove").
> ¹ To remove
### gük
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋyk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋyk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋyk]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gǖk|*gǖk]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gaw|*gaw]]_ ("north-easterly wind") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ek|*-ek]]_ ("animate object nominaliser").
> ¹ North-easterly wind
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#gík|gík]]_
# h
### habom
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑbom]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑbɔ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χäbɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hapum|*hapum]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ha-|*ha-]]_ ("progressive") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pum|*pum]]_ ("ripe").
> ¹ To ripen
### haim
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑim]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑjm]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χäjm]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hayīm|*hayīm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hüy|*hüy]]_ ("rest") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Bed; ² Bedroom, personal quarters
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#hen|hen]]_
### hamog
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑmoŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmɔ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χämɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hamug|*hamug]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ha-|*ha-]]_ ("progressive") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mug|*mug]]_ ("try, attempt").
> ¹ To keep trying, working towards something
### hamök'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑmøkʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χämœkʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hamük'|*hamük']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ha-|*ha-]]_ ("progressive") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mük'|*mük']]_ ("age").
> ¹ To grow old
### hamök'et
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑmøkʼet]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœkʼɛt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χämœkʼɛt]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hamük'et|*hamük'et]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hamük'|*hamük']]_ ("to grow old") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Old person
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#hanket|hanket]]_
### hamöl
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑmøl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χämew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hamül|*hamül]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ha-|*ha-]]_ ("progressive") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mül|*mül]]_ ("learn, teach").
> ¹ To develop a skill; ² To learn something
### hamön
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑmøn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χämɔ̃ː]

> ¹ To grow; ² To develop
### hamöx
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑmøʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χämœʃ]

### hanim

### hia

### hilap'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [xilɑpʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [xiɫpʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [xewpʼ]

> ¹ [[Hilap']], a particular species of [[Sibig]] which stands on two legs and has opposable thumbs

### hiwhiw

> ¹ To breathe

### holaq

*v.* From [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#fara’e|fara’e]]_ ("to burn, cook"), from _[[Xiri dictionary#fa-|fa-]]_ ("verb prefix") + _[[Xiri dictionary#rha’e|rha’e]]_ ("fire").
> ¹ To cook

### honu

*v.* Perhaps related to [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#furu|furu]]_ ("to make, mold").
> ¹ To create
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#honuta|honuta]]_ ("artificial")
### honuta
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɸonʊdʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɸonʊdə]

### hoqaw
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɸoʔʌw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɸoʔäw]

### höe
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [xʷøe]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɸøɛ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɸøə]

### hyac'ek

### ibib

### ica
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [itʃɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [idʒʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [idʒə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔica|*ʔica]]_ ("wide"), from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔic|*ʔic]]_ ("wide, broad").
> ¹ Long
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íja|íja]]_
### icab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [itʃɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [idʒʌb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [idʒʌb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔicap|*ʔicap]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔic|*ʔic]]_ ("wide, broad") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ap|*ap]]_ ("lay out, arrange").
> ¹ To lay out flat; ² To position far apart
### icaqa
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [idʒʌʔʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [idʒʌʔə]

*stat.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#ici|ici]]_ ("pig").
> ¹ Fat, as of a person
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íca|íca]]_
### ichamön
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [itʃχɑmøn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [itʃχʌmœ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [itʃχʌmɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔichamyün|*ʔichamyün]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔic'-|*ʔic'-]]_ ("upwards") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hamyün|*hamyün]]_ ("to grow, develop").
> ¹ To grow, as of a plant
### ici
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [idʒɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [idʒɪ]

*n.* From [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#iji|iji]]_, from [[Proto-Xiric language|Proto-Xiric]] _[[Proto-Xiric dictionary#\*eici|*eici]]_.
> ¹ Pig
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#icaqa|icaqa]]_ ("fat")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íji|íji]]_
### icköc
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [itʃkøtʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [itʃkœtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [itʃkœtʃ]

### ic'ik'

> ¹ Intestines
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ken|ken]]_
### kale

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qwǖk|*qwǖk]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qwiw|*qwiw]]_ ("south-easterly monsoon wind") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ek|*-ek]]_ ("animate object nominaliser").
> ¹ South-easterly monsoon wind
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kík|kík]]_
### kükü
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kykʏ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kykʏ]

*n.* From [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#kwi|kwi]]_ ("yam"), from [[Proto-Xiric language|Proto-Xiric]] _[[Proto-Xiric dictionary#\*kue|*kue]]_.
> ¹ Tuber; ² Yam
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#cikü|cikü]]_ ("red potato")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíkö|kíkö]]_
### kwilta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kwiltɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kwiɫdʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kwewdə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kwilta|*kwilta]]_, Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kil|*kil]]_ ("tired, bored").
> ¹ Lazy
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#köda|köda]]_
### kyahyac'

### k'abah
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑbɑχ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑbʌχ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼäbʌχ]

> ¹ The mountains of [[T'ugü]]'
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#k'abahcüw|k'abahcüw]]_ ("öxp'a")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kabah|kabah]]_
### k'abahcüw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑbɑχtʃyw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑbʌχtʃʏw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼäbʌχtʃew]

*n.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#k'abah|k'abah]]_ ("mountains") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#cüw|cüw]]_ ("cüo").
> ¹ A large wug, similar to terrestrial takin
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kabahcö|kabahcö]]_
### k'abk'ab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑbqʼɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑbqʼʌb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼäbqʼʌb]

> ¹ Any sea mollusc with an external shell
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kapkab|kapkab]]_

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'apk'ap|*k'apk'ap]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'ap|*k'ap]]_ ("sweat") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("directionless intransitive").

### k'ak'ohümi
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑkʼoxʷymi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑkʼɔɸʏmɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼäkʼɔɸʏmɪ]

*n.* From [[High Alöbi]] _[[High Alöbi dictionary#q'aq'ugǖmi|q'aq'ugǖmi]]_, from _[[High Alöbi dictionary#q'aq'ug|q'aq'ug]]_ ("giant snail") + _[[High Alöbi dictionary#ǖm|ǖm]]_ ("wooden construction") + _[[High Alöbi dictionary#-i|-i]]_ ("relational linker"). Equivalent to _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#t'ak'og|t'ak'og]]_ ("giant snail") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#üm|üm]]_ ("wooden construction") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#-i|-i]]_ ("relational linker").
> ¹ A large wagon which can be inverted to form a temporary home, used in [[Öb#Seasonal migration|Öb seasonal migrations]]
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kakofmi|kakofmi]]_

### k'imay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼimɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼimʌj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼimäj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'imay|*k'imay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'i-|*k'i-]]_ ("again") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*may|*may]]_ ("know, remember").
> ¹ To remember
### k'iwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼiwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼiwʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼiwə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'iwa|*k'iwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'i|*k'i]]_ ("hang, swing") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Hanging
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíva|kíva]]_
### k'iwk'iw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼiwkʼiw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼiwkʼɪw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼewkʼew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'iwk'iw|*k'iwk'iw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'iw|*k'iw]]_ ("cry") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("directionless intransitive").
> ¹ To cry
### k'ixam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼiʃɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼiʃʌ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼiʃɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'ixam|*k'ixam]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xam|*xam]]_ ("throw").
> ¹ Spear
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíxon|kíxon]]_
### k'labklix
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼlɑbkliʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼlɑbklɪʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼläbklɪʃ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'laptlix|*k'laptlix]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'lap'|*q'lap']]_ ("lightning, thunder") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*p'atlix|*p'atlix]]_ ("bright flash of light").
> ¹ Electrical storm; ² Lightning strike
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#klapklix|klapklix]]_
### k'unön
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼunøn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼunœ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼunɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'ūnün|*k'ūnün]]_.
> ¹ A plant whose roots are used to make the spice [[K'unön#K'ilunön|k'ilunön']]
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kúnon|kúnon]]_
### k'übi
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼybi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼybɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼybɪ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'ǖpi|*k'ǖpi]]_.
> ¹ [[K'übi]], a small domesticated ungulate kept as livestock, similar to duikers
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíbi|kíbi]]_
### k'winoa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼwinoɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼwinɔʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼwinɔə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'winua|*q'winua]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'win|*q'win]]_ ("dark") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Dark
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kvínova|kvínova]]_
### k'winta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼwintɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼwɪ̃ndʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼwɪ̃ndə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'winta|*q'winta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'win|*q'win]]_ ("dark") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Dark; ² Dull, blunt
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kvinda|kvinda]]_
# l
### labet
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑbet]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑbɛt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [läbɛt]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rapet|*rapet]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rap|*rap]]_ ("bind, restrain") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Bundle (of sticks); ² Clump of bamboo
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#labet|labet]]_
### labina
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑbinɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑbɪnʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [läbɪnə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rapina|*rapina]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ra|*ra]]_ ("smell, taste") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pin|*pin]]_ ("bitter").
> ¹ Bitter; ² Unripe
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#labna|labna]]_
### lablah
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑblɑχ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑblʌχ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [läblʌχ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*glaplah|*glaplah]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*glap|*glap]]_ ("star cluster").
> ¹ The dense cluster of stars at the core of the globular cluster
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lablah|lablah]]_
### laibem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑibem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑjbɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [läjbɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*layipem|*layipem]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lip|*lip]]_ ("trap") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Pitfall trap
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#leben|leben]]_
### lakawa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑqɑwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑqʌwʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [läqʌwə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rakawa|*rakawa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ra|*ra]]_ ("smell, taste") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kaw|*kaw]]_ ("urine").
> ¹ Smelling of urine
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lakva|lakva]]_
### lakig
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑkiŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑkɪ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [läkɪ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rakig|*rakig]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ra|*ra]]_ ("smell, taste") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kig|*kig]]_ ("excrement").
> ¹ Smell of excrement
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lakin|lakin]]_
### lakwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑkwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑkwʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [läkwə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rakwa|*rakwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ra|*ra]]_ ("smell, taste").
> ¹ Foul-smelling
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lakva|lakva]]_
### lak'em
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑkʼem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑkʼɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [läkʼɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lak'em|*lak'em]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lak'|*lak']]_ ("insert") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Plug, cork
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#laken|laken]]_
### -lam

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-lam|*-lam]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count flat, stackable objects such as flatbreads, leaves and pieces of cloth
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-lon|-lon]]_
### lamüa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑmyɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑmʏʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lämʏə]

> ¹ Sweet
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lamöya|lamöya]]_

ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lʌ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lɔ̃ː]

*prep.*
> ¹ Comitative
### lanog
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑnoŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑnɔ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [länɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ranug|*ranug]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ra|*ra]]_ ("smell, taste") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nug|*nug]]_ ("taste, try").
> ¹ To smell; ² To taste
### laqaka
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑʔɑqɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑʔʌqʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [läʔʌqə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*raqaka|*raqaka]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ra|*ra]]_ ("smell, taste") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qak|*qak]]_ ("putrid").
> ¹ Putrid
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#laka|laka]]_, [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#rha’aga|rha’aga]]_
### laqem
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑʔɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [läʔɛ̃ː]

*n.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#holaq|holaq]]_ ("to cook") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#-em|-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Cooked food
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#laqen|laqen]]_
### laqtaqa
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑʔtʌʔʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [läʔtʌʔə]

### latoga
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑtoɴɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑdɔɴʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lädɔɴə]

### latüxa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑtyʃɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑdʏʃʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lädʏʃə]

### lat'aga

### laüm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑjm]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [läjm]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*layǖm|*layǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lǖm|*lǖm]]_ ("affix, fasten").
> ¹ Joint, as between pieces of wood; ² Corner
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#len|len]]_
### lawic
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑwitʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑwtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [läwtʃ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rawic|*rawic]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*raw|*raw]]_ ("sew, weave") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ic|*-ic]]_ ("agentive").

### laxöw

### leqic

### leqmok

### libic

### liblib

### lihas
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [liχʌs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [liχʌs]

*n.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#amlih|amlih]]_ ("to point at"). Perhaps related to [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#haskāzi|haskāzi]]_ ("arrow").
> ¹ Arrow
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#líhas|líhas]]_
### lihwel
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lixʷel]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [liɸɛɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [liɸew]

> ¹ To measure a length
### lilaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lilɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lilʌw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [liläw]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rilaw|*rilaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<il>|*<il>]]_ ("result or product") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*raw|*raw]]_ ("sew, weave").
> ¹ Linen cloth
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lílo|lílo]]_ ("cloth, sail") → [[Ahōtoli]] _[[Ahōtoli dictionary#lilō|lilō]]_ ("sail of a ship")
### lisem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lisem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lisɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lisɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lisem|*lisem]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lis|*lis]]_ ("light") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Point of light
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lísen|lísen]]_
### liswin
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [liswin]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [liswɪ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [liswɪ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lisgwin|*lisgwin]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lis|*lis]]_ ("light") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gwin|*gwin]]_ ("eclipse").
> ¹ A solar eclipse by either of the two moons of Winter
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lísvin|lísvin]]_
### lökic
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [løkitʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [løkɪtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [løkɪtʃ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lükic|*lükic]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lük|*lük]]_ ("poke") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ic|*-ic]]_ ("agentive").
> ¹ Any wader bird with a long thin bill
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lökic|lökic]]_
### löktek'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [løktekʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [løktɛkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [løktɛkʼ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lükteq'|*lükteq']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lük|*lük]]_ ("poke") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*teq'|*teq']]_ ("claw").
> ¹ The claw of a [[Ciblökog]]
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#löktek|löktek]]_
### lötoa

> ¹ New, as of objects
### löxök'

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lüxük'|*lüxük']]_, Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lǖx|*lǖx]]_ ("white"), [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cuq'|*cuq']]_ ("stone").
> ¹ Chalk
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#löxök|löxök]]_
### lubic

### lublub

> ¹ A calendar year, equal to 250 days
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ñomö|ñomö]]_
# n
### -na

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-na|*-na]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count longish objects such as fish (dead, for eating), certain fruit, dead bodies, knives and planks of wood
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-na|-na]]_

### nayam

### nayaqem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nɑjɑʔem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nɑjʔɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [näjʔɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nayaqem|*nayaqem]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*naq|*naq]]_ ("eat") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Feast hall
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#neqen|neqen]]_
### naynay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nɑjnɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nɑjnʌj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [näjnäj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*naynay|*naynay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nay|*nay]]_ ("think") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("directionless intransitive").
> ¹ To think
### nayol
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nɑjol]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nɑjɔɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [näjow]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nayur|*nayur]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nur|*nur]]_ ("dream").
> ¹ Dream
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#neyú|neyú]]_
### necwi
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [netʃwi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nedʒwɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [nedʒwɪ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*necwi|*necwi]]_.
> ¹ [[Necwi]], small feathered dinosaur
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#nijvi|nijvi]]_
### neheb
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [nexeb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [nexɛb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [nexɛb]

> ¹ To drink
### neqoa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [neʔoɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [neʔɔʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [neʔɔə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nequa|*nequa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*neq|*neq]]_ ("old") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Old, as of objects
### neqom
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [neʔom]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [neʔɔ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [neʔɔ̃ː]

> ¹ Antique, old artifact
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#niqon|niqon]]_

> ¹ Human plural

### nühö

### oban

> ¹ To fill up; ² To pour

### olak'

### olaw

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wuraw|*wuraw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wu-|*wu-]]_ ("back and forth") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*raw|*raw]]_ ("sew, weave").
> ¹ To weave
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#uro|uro]]_
### olay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [olɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [olʌj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [oläj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wray|*wray]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*we-|*we-]]_ ("absence of") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ray|*ray]]_ ("be in a place").
> ¹ To be absent

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*uray|*uray]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*u-|*u-]]_ ("causative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ray|*ray]]_ ("be in a place").
> ¹ To put in place

### omö

> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#acowmö|acowmö]]_ ("six"), _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#wibowmö|wibowmö]]_ ("seven"), _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#nüɸowmö|nüɸowmö]]_ ("eight"), _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#bixowmö|bixowmö]]_ ("nine")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#umö|umö]]_

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ummü|*ummü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*um|*um]]_ ("five") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mü|*mü]]_ ("cycle").
> ¹ A major month, equal to 50 days
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-ö|-ö]]_ ("cycle classifier"), [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#umö|umö]]_

# ö
### -ö

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mü|*mü]]_ ("cycle"), from [[Proto-Upic language|Proto-Upic]] _[[Proto-Upic dictionary#\*mu|*mu]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count cyclic objects such as wheels, months and years, as well as generations and things of a reciprocal nature such as transactions
### öb

### öhnim

### qaywiw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔɑjwiw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑjwɪw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔäjwew]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qaywiw|*qaywiw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qwiw|*qwiw]]_ ("south-easterly monsoon wind").
> ¹ Monsoon season
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#qevö|qevö]]_
### qayxil
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔɑjʃil]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑjʃɪɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔäjʃew]

> ¹ To bury
### qelqel
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔelʔel]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔeɫʔɛɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔewʔew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qerqer|*qerqer]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qer|*qer]]_ ("close eyes") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("directionless intransitive").
> ¹ To close the eyes
### quta
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔudʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔudə]

*stat.* From [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#a’uda|a’uda]]_ ("power"), from [[Proto-Xiric language|Proto-Xiric]] _[[Proto-Xiric dictionary#\*a’uta|*a’uta]]_.
> ¹ Strong; ² Powerful
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#qúda|qúda]]_
### qütoa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔytoɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔydɔʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔydɔə]

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#qídva|qídva]]_

### tibtib
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tibtib]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tibdɪb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tibdɪb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tīptīp|*tīptīp]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tīp|*tīp]]_ ("neck") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Neck
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#díbdib|díbdib]]_
### ticok'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [titʃokʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tidʒɔkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tidʒɔkʼ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tīcuq'|*tīcuq']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tī-|*tī-]]_ ("body part") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cuq'|*cuq']]_ ("stone").
> ¹ Testicle
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#díjok|díjok]]_
### tic'ab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [titʃʼɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [titʃʼʌb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [titʃʼʌb]

### tihac
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tiχɑtʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tiχʌtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tiχʌtʃ]

### tikis

### tiköm

### -tik'

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-tik'|*-tik']]_.

### tilös

### tyomta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [comtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [cɔ̃ndʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [cɔ̃ndə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tyumta|*tyumta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tyum|*tyum]]_ ("curl up") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Curled up
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#jönda|jönda]]_
### tyomtyag
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [comcɑɴ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [cɔ̃ɲɟʌ̃ɴ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [cɔ̃ɲɟɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tyumtyag|*tyumtyag]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tyum|*tyum]]_ ("curl up") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tyag|*tyag]]_ ("bone").
> ¹ Curved horn of certain ungulates
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#jönjon|jönjon]]_
# t'

### uböt
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ubøt]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ubœt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ubœt]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūppüt|*ūppüt]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūp-|*ūp-]]_ ("surface") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*püt|*püt]]_ ("paint").
> ¹ To paint
### ubsöb
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ubsøb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ubsœb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ubsœb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūpsüp|*ūpsüp]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūp-|*ūp-]]_ ("surface") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*süp|*süp]]_ ("carve").
> ¹ To carve, scratch a line
### ubt'ab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ubtʼɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ubtʼʌb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ubtʼʌb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūpt'ap|*ūpt'ap]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūp-|*ūp-]]_ ("surface") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ap|*t'ap]]_ ("smooth").
> ¹ To smooth out
### ubt'ik
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ubtʼik]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ubtʼɪk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ubtʼɪk]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūpt'ik|*ūpt'ik]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūp-|*ūp-]]_ ("surface") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ik|*t'ik]]_ ("cut").
> ¹ To shave
### ubxak'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ubʃɑqʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ubʃʌqʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ubʃʌqʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūpxak'|*ūpxak']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūp-|*ūp-]]_ ("surface") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xak'|*xak']]_ ("pound").
> ¹ To pound flat
### ugo
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [uŋo]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [uŋɔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [uŋɔ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūgu|*ūgu]]_.
> ¹ [[Ugo]], a large domesticated ungulate used as a draft animal, similar to cattle
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#úgo|úgo]]_
### -uk

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ūk|*-ūk]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count objects with a branching structure such as trees, pieces of [[Cimcim#Ökya cimcim|ökya cimcim]] and lightning bolts
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-uk|-uk]]_
### utok
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [utok]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [udɔk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [udɔk]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūtuk|*ūtuk]]_.
> ¹ Lizard, salamander
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#údok|údok]]_
# ü
### üa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖa|*ǖa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ|*ǖ]]_ ("wood, wooden").
> ¹ Wooden
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íya|íya]]_
### üal
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yɑl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yʌɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yäw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖʔal|*ǖʔal]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔal|*ʔal]]_ ("outside").
> ¹ To be outside of
### übaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ybɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ybʌw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ybäw]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yǖpaw|*yǖpaw]]_.
> ¹ Gourd
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íbo|íbo]]_
### ücal
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ytʃɑl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ydʒʌɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ydʒäw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖcal|*ǖcal]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cal|*cal]]_ ("boundary").
> ¹ To be enclosed within
### ücel
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ytʃel]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ydʒɛɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ydʒew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖcer|*ǖcer]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cer|*cer]]_ ("end").
> ¹ To be at the edge of
### ücik'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ytʃikʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ydʒɪkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ydʒɪkʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖcīk'|*ǖcīk']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cīk'|*cīk']]_ ("tip").
> ¹ To be at the tip of
### ühüm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yxʷym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yɸʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yɸʊ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖhǖm|*ǖhǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hǖm|*hǖm]]_ ("upstream of, before").
> ¹ To be uphill, upstream of; ² To be before
### ükis
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ykis]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ykɪs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ykɪs]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖkīs|*ǖkīs]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kīs|*kīs]]_ ("top, on top").
> ¹ To be on top of
### ük'at
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yqʼɑt]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yqʼʌt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yqʼʌt]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖk'at|*ǖk'at]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'at|*k'at]]_ ("base, bottom part").
> ¹ To be at the bottom of
### ülab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ylɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yɫb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ewb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖnrap|*ǖnrap]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖn-|*ǖn-]]_ ("slowly and carefully") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rap|*rap]]_ ("bind, restrain").
> ¹ To bind firmly together
### ülan
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ylɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ylʌ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ylɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖran|*ǖran]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ran|*ran]]_ ("on"). Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖtyan|*ǖtyan]]_ ("near"), [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖyan|*ǖyan]]_ ("inside").
> ¹ To be on the surface of
### ülap'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ylɑpʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yɫpʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ewpʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖnlap'|*ǖnlap']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖn-|*ǖn-]]_ ("slowly and carefully") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lap'|*lap']]_ ("grab, snatch").
> ¹ To take into the hand; ² To grab onto
### ülay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ylɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ylʌj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yläj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖray|*ǖray]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ray|*ray]]_ ("be in a place").
> ¹ To be at a place
### üm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʊ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖm|*ǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ|*ǖ]]_ ("wood, wooden") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ A complex construction made from several pieces of wood
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#k'ak'ohümi|k'ak'ohümi]]_ ("wagon house")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#un|un]]_
### ümüm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ymym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ymʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ymʊ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yǖmyǖm|*yǖmyǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yǖm|*yǖm]]_ ("container, pot") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Container, pot
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ímun|ímun]]_
### üncaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yntʃɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʏ̃ndʒʌw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʊ̃ndʒäw]

> ¹ To physically deform

### üntil
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yntil]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʏ̃ndɪɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʊ̃ndew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖntil|*ǖntil]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖn-|*ǖn-]]_ ("slowly and carefully") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*til|*til]]_ ("approach").
> ¹ To approach carefully, as when hunting an animal
### ünü
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yny]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ynʏ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ynʏ]

### üqüt

### üta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ytɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ydʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ydə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yǖta|*yǖta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yaw|*yaw]]_ ("enclose") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Enclosed
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ída|ída]]_

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yǖta|*yǖta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yaw|*yaw]]_ ("bend") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Bent, curved
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#üt|üt]]_ ("bow")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ída|ída]]_
### ütöl
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ytøl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ydœɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ydew]

### ütyan
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ycɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yɟʌ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yɟɔ̃ː]

> ¹ To be within reach; ² To be directly next to

### üxöm

### üxt'ak'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yʃtʼɑqʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yʃtʼʌqʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yʃtʼʌqʼ]

### üyal
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yjɑl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yjʌɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yjäw]

> ¹ To be in the middle of
### üyan
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yjɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yjʌ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yjɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖyan|*ǖyan]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yan|*yan]]_ ("within, inside"). Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖran|*ǖran]]_ ("on"), [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖtyan|*ǖtyan]]_ ("near").
> ¹ To be inside of
### üyet'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [yjetʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yjtʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ejtʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖyet'|*ǖyet']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yat'|*yat']]_ ("fear").
> ¹ To fear

### -w

> ¹ Stativiser
### waba
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [wɑbɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [wɑbʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [wäbə]

> ¹ Easy; ² Light weight
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#vaba|vaba]]_
### waca

### wacam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [wɑtʃɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [wɑdʒʌ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [wädʒɔ̃ː]

### wack'ic
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [wɑtʃkʼitʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [wɑtʃkʼɪtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [wätʃkʼɪtʃ]

> ¹ Comet
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#vackic|vackic]]_
### wacoa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [wɑtʃoɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [wɑdʒɔʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [wädʒɔə]

> ¹ Far away
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#vajva|vajva]]_

### waik'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [wɑikʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [wɑjkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [wäjkʼ]

### walag
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [wɑlʌ̃ɴ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [wälɔ̃ː]

> ¹ Yam wine

### wamcal

### wemay

### wibmyawmü
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [wibmjɑwmy]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [wimjʌwmʏ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [wimjäwmʏ]

> ¹ Fifty

### wisa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [wisɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [wisʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [wisə]

### xi=

*procl.*
> ¹ Animate plural
### xigoa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃiŋoɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃiŋɔʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃiŋɔə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xigua|*xigua]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xig|*xig]]_ ("sickness, ailment") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Sick
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xígova|xígova]]_
### xigob
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃiŋob]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃiŋɔb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃiŋɔb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xigup|*xigup]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xig|*xig]]_ ("sickness, ailment") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ep|*-ep]]_ ("person object nominaliser").
> ¹ Sick person
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xígob|xígob]]_
### xilak'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃilɑqʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃiɫqʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃewqʼ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xilak'|*xilak']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<il>|*<il>]]_ ("result or product") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xak'|*xak']]_ ("pound").
> ¹ Pâté
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xök|xök]]_
### xilbö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃilbø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃiɫbœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃewbœ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xilpü|*xilpü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xil|*xil]]_ ("bury") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pü|*pü]]_ ("vegetable").
> ¹ Root vegetable, tuber
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xöbö|xöbö]]_
### xilub
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃilub]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃiɫb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃewb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xilūp|*xilūp]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<il>|*<il>]]_ ("result or product") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xūp|*xūp]]_ ("adze").
> ¹ Dugout canoe
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xöb|xöb]]_
### xlicek
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃlitʃek]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃlidʒɛk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃlidʒɛk]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xlicek|*xlicek]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xlic|*xlic]]_ ("writhe") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ek|*-ek]]_ ("animate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Eel; ² Worm
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xlíjek|xlíjek]]_
### xocat
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃodʒʌt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃodʒʌt]

*n.* From [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#fawē’eyažožāda|fawē’eyažožāda]]_, from _[[Xiri dictionary#fawē’e|fawē’e]]_ ("to break, attack") + _[[Xiri dictionary#-ya|-ya]]_ ("momentane marker") + _[[Xiri dictionary#xožāda|xožāda]]_ ("root").
> ¹ Garlic
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xujat|xujat]]_
### xoka
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃoqɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃoqʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃoqə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xuka|*xuka]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xuk|*xuk]]_ ("crumble").
> ¹ Powdery
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xuka|xuka]]_
### xola
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃolɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃolʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃolə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xura|*xura]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xur|*xur]]_ ("float on water").
> ¹ Buoyant
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xula|xula]]_
### xolüm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃolym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃolʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃolʊ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xurǖm|*xurǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xur|*xur]]_ ("float on water") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖm|*ǖm]]_ ("wooden construction").
> ¹ Raft
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xulun|xulun]]_
### xolxol
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃolʃol]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃoɫʃɔɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃowʃow]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xurxur|*xurxur]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xur|*xur]]_ ("float on water") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("directionless intransitive").
> ¹ To float
### xonoa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃonoɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃonɔʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃonɔə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xunua|*xunua]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xun|*xun]]_ ("obscure") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Obscured; ² Not visible; ³ Hard to understand
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xunova|xunova]]_
### xoyxoy
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃojʃoj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃojʃɔj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃojʃoj]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xuyxuy|*xuyxuy]]_, Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*si|*si]]_ ("water"), [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'ay|*q'ay]]_ ("deep").
> ¹ Deep water
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xíxí|xíxí]]_
### xöga
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃøɴɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃøɴʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃøɴə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xüga|*xüga]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xüg|*xüg]]_ ("soft").
> ¹ Soft
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xöga|xöga]]_, [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#xoga|xoga]]_
### xömoa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃømoɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃømɔʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃømɔə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xümua|*xümua]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xüm|*xüm]]_ ("downstream of, before") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Downstream; ² Later
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xömova|xömova]]_

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xümua|*xümua]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xüm|*xüm]]_ ("hide") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Hidden; ² Unknown
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xömova|xömova]]_
### xömom
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃømom]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃømɔ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃømɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xümum|*xümum]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xüm|*xüm]]_ ("downstream of, before") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Later point; ² Successor
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xömon|xömon]]_

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xümum|*xümum]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xüm|*xüm]]_ ("hide") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Something unknown
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xömon|xömon]]_
### xömxöm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃømʃøm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃœ̃nʃœ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃɔ̃ːʃɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xümxüm|*xümxüm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xüm|*xüm]]_ ("hide") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("directionless intransitive").
> ¹ To hide; ² To store
### xubxub
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃubʃub]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃubʃʊb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃubʃʊb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xūpxūp|*xūpxūp]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xūp|*xūp]]_ ("adze") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("repetitively").
> ¹ To scrape out material, as with an adze
### xulab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃulɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃuɫb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃowb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xūrap|*xūrap]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xū-|*xū-]]_ ("round in circles") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rap|*rap]]_ ("bind, restrain").
> ¹ To tie into a bundle; ² To wrap around tightly
### xun=

*procl.*
> ¹ Inanimate plural
### xuniw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃuniw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃunɪw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃunew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xūnyiw|*xūnyiw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xū-|*xū-]]_ ("round in circles") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nyiw|*nyiw]]_ ("twist, twine").
> ¹ To twist
### xunüb
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃunyb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃunʏb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃunʏb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xūnǖp|*xūnǖp]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xū-|*xū-]]_ ("round in circles") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nǖp|*nǖp]]_ ("wrap").
> ¹ To wrap around; ² To bend round
### xutay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃutɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃudʌj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃudäj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xūtay|*xūtay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xū-|*xū-]]_ ("round in circles") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tay|*tay]]_ ("move").
> ¹ To orbit; ² To move in circles
### xutyom
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃucom]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃuɟɔ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃuɟɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xūtyum|*xūtyum]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xū-|*xū-]]_ ("round in circles") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tyum|*tyum]]_ ("curl up").
> ¹ To curve, curl round
### xuyaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃujɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃujʌw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃujäw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xūyaw|*xūyaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xū-|*xū-]]_ ("round in circles") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yaw|*yaw]]_ ("bend").
> ¹ To bend, curve
### xücaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃytʃɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃydʒʌw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃydʒäw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xǖcaw|*xǖcaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*caw|*caw]]_ ("deform").
> ¹ To stretch
### xület
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃylet]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃyɫt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃewt]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xǖlet|*xǖlet]]_.
> ¹ A large acidic berry
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xöt|xöt]]_
### xwia
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃwiɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃwiʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃwiə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xwia|*xwia]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xwi|*xwi]]_ ("bad").
> ¹ Bad, evil
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xvíya|xvíya]]_
### xwita
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʃwitɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʃwidʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʃwidə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xwita|*xwita]]_.
> ¹ Drunk
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#xvída|xvída]]_
# y
### yabek
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑbek]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑbɛk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jäbɛk]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yapek|*yapek]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yap|*yap]]_ ("squeeze") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ek|*-ek]]_ ("animate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Insect larva
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yabek|yabek]]_, [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#yaba|yaba]]_
### yabsiw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑbsiw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑbsɪw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jäbsew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yapsiw|*yapsiw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yap|*yap]]_ ("squeeze") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*siw|*siw]]_ ("extract").
> ¹ To squeeze out juice
### yabta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑbtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑbdʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jäbdə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yapta|*yapta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yap|*yap]]_ ("close, as of a mouth") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Closed, as of a mouth
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yabda|yabda]]_ ("folded")
### yacoa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑtʃoɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑdʒɔʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jädʒɔə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yacua|*yacua]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yac|*yac]]_ ("joy") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Happy
### yac'oa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑtʃʼoɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑtʃʼɔʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jätʃʼɔə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yac'ua|*yac'ua]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yac'|*yac']]_ ("anger") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Angry
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yacva|yacva]]_
### yaloa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑloɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑlɔʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jälɔə]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yarua|*yarua]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yar|*yar]]_ ("central, in the middle") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Central
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yalova|yalova]]_
### yaloc
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑlotʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑɫtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jäwtʃ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yaruc|*yaruc]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ruc|*ruc]]_ ("loc").
> ¹ A non-physical part of the self, similar to the soul
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yoc|yoc]]_
### yam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jʌ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yam|*yam]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yar|*yar]]_ ("central, in the middle") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Middle part
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yon|yon]]_
### yanip'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑnipʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑnɪpʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jänɪpʼ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yanip'|*yanip']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<an>|*<an>]]_ ("instrument") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yip'|*yip']]_ ("pinch, squeeze").
> ¹ Tongs
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yanip|yanip]]_
### yanyo
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑɲo]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑɲɔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jäɲɔ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yanyu|*yanyu]]_.
> ¹ [[Yanyo]], a crane which migrates between [[T'ugü]] and the [[Haankaysiw Steppe]]
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yaño|yaño]]_
### yaöxem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑøʃem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑjʃɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jäjʃɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yayüxem|*yayüxem]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yüx|*yüx]]_ ("heat") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Hot spring
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yexen|yexen]]_
### yaq
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑʔ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑʔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jäʔ]

> ¹ To scratch; ² To gnaw at
### yata

### yaten

### yat'oa

### yawcal

### yaxa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑʃɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑʃʌ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jäʃə]

### yaxeb
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jɑʃeb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jɑʃɛb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jäʃɛb]

### yaya

### yeqic

### yeqicog

### yomih

### yup'üh

### yuso

### yuyu
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [juju]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jujʊ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jujʊ]
